I stayed for four consecutive days, so it must be very cost-effective. The Holiday Inn Shanghai Pudong Greenland made me very moved and unforgettable.

1. Customer service is in-depth and considerate
We haven‚Äôt traveled for four years after the epidemic. One of the two suitcases we carried couldn‚Äôt open the lock and one forgot the password. After hearing our appeal, the account manager Simon and the friends in the lobby assisted us without damaging the structure. Solve this difficult problem. We wanted to leave a tip and said that this is what they should do. The very good attitude also showed professionalism and patience in listening to customer needs that ordinary services cannot.

2. The shuttle bus route is thoughtfully arranged
The hotel provides scheduled shuttle buses to Disneyland and People's Square, allowing guests to make full use of transportation resources. When checking in, the account manager will ask the receptionist to provide a dedicated WeChat account. Customers can book shuttle buses and ask questions about their stay in the hotel through online interaction, which is very considerate. The shuttle bus driver is also very dedicated. During the journey and before arriving at the destination, he will clearly explain the stop of the subsequent shuttle bus and publicly contact the driver's phone number for the convenience of guests. Because we were delayed on our return trip to Disneyland, we also contacted the driver. , ended up being five minutes late, thank you Mr. Driver for waiting and other passengers for your tolerance.

3. A rich hotel breakfast was prepared for us in advance
We have breakfast every day in the restaurant on the first floor. The restaurant manager George comes to take care of the dining situation every day. When the shuttle bus time is tight, he can also call the restaurant hotline through the guest room and ask the chef to help us prepare omelet eggs and wonton noodles in advance. You can eat immediately when you come down and take a seat. Other facilities such as coffee and salad are also quite sufficient, allowing guests to have more choices.

Looking for a professional, considerate, comfortable and cost-effective Disney travel hotel, Holiday Inn Shanghai Pudong Greenland is definitely your first choice.

msg:4.24 at 5 pm the housekeeping aunt came in to clean. There was a cell phone on the bed. I was putting on makeup and my partner was on the sofa. Everyone was doing their own things. Then when the housekeeping aunt was changing the sheets, she wrapped up the phone on the bed and put it in the linen cart. Afterwards, I asked the aunt if she had shaken it to check if there was anything inside the sheets. The aunt also said no. Then my partner and I went out at 8 pm and came back at 10 pm. When we were getting ready to go to bed in the early morning, we found that my partner's other iPhone 14promax was missing. We immediately called the manager on duty, but the other party said that it was absolutely impossible that someone from their hotel had taken it. Their attitude was just so-so and they didn't seem to want to help us solve the problem. It was very speechless. The police came the next day and asked the aunt about the situation at that time. The aunt meant that she didn't check the sheets in her hand at that time. Anyway, she just rolled them into a ball and put them in the linen cart. Then the aunt went off work. In the end, the employees of a third-party company that cleans the linens came and pushed the linen cart away. I'm too lazy to say more about the rest. The phone was 100% in the linen cart. If it wasn't in the linen cart or if it fell somewhere, it would have been picked up by someone. Why couldn't the aunt check it at that time? Besides, we were traveling as customers. When the housekeeping department came to clean, could we not put our phones on the bed? ??? ??? ??? Very funny. Now the hotel has been blaming the police station and refusing to compensate us. It is really funny. They also repeatedly asked my partner and I if we really put our phones on the bed? ??? Most importantly, why did we have to direct and act out this scene of dropping our phones? ??? ??? ??? Finally, I want to tell everyone to avoid this hotel under the InterContinental Group. The management is not in place! What did my partner and I do wrong? We just wanted to travel to Shanghai and eat delicious food, but our phones were left on the bed. We went out to eat and when we came back, our phones were gone. Did the aunt come in and change the sheets halfway through? ??? Everyone, open your eyes! ! This hotel is really unreliable! ! ! ! ! ! ! ! ! My partner also bought the phone on JD.com for more than 8,000 yuan!
